電影專刊美國的電影刋物是否盡是公司或明星們的宣傳工具？  密齊　　（一）是的方面（下）　　不過有的時候，那位宣傳專家没有這許多不同的故事，去散佈給許多電影雜誌，於是她們迫不得已，就將同樣的故事，送給兩家，或多家互相競爭的雜誌了。所以我們常常在幾家不同的雜誌裏，發見相同的文章和照相。我們承認，電影雜誌裏的相片，是一種美術品，是對於美國藝術的一個貢獻。它們在電影雜誌裏所佔的空白地位，至少有一半之多，並且是電影雜誌的最重要的一部分。猶之文章可以相同，相片在電影雜誌裏，亦是可以相同的。其主要的原因。就是因爲他們是從一個地方發出來的。有人曾隨手檢了十一月份的十種不同的電影雜誌。他發見了有兩本是封面圖書相同的，每一本裏都有一幀相同的，梅蕙絲的照相。有兩張相同的照片的，共有八本。有五張相同的照片的，共六本；而有八張相同的照片裏有三本。　　以上所說的無稽空談，宣傳文字和照相，就是電影雜誌所不可缺的三大要素。除此之外，還有許多其他的次要標目。第一，我們可以提到它們裏面常常登載的「美容術」（Ｂeauty　hints）這種文字，或是標明某某明星寫的，或是叙述某某明星的美容方法的，美國全國，無論男女，喜觀看的人很多。這種美容術表面是敎人怎樣修飾他們的面容，或是操練他們的身體。其實呢，副作用很多。一來可以替明星們宣傳，間接的替公司方面推廣營業；二則那種文章裏所提到的什麽什麽化妝品，大都是在它們雜誌裏登載鉅幅廣告的東西。還有一門，呌做「時裝」（Ｓtyles）。他們也是替明星們宣傳的工具。並且推廣了某某裁衣以司的新式樣，或是某種衣料。這於電影雜誌廣告方面，當然也不能說没有關係。第三就是「影評」（Ｒevlews）。各家電影雜誌，都有它們的影評人，便是它們裏面的評，總是千遍一律，祇往好裏講，不往壞裏說。據說在二百個評裏面，祗有一個評，是眞正用批評的眼光來寫的。當然，無論什麽片子總有　它一部份精彩的地方，於是影評者就利用了這點，去誘惑一般觀衆了。第四是「讀者通信」（Ｌetters　From　the　readers）。普通係有奬的。它們的文章，亦是萬口同聲的對於影片或影星們界歌頌揄揚。第五是競賽或選舉（Ｃontests）。差不多什麽雜誌裏，都有一種競賽的舉行，至少每年一次。這種競賽有兩種顯著的用意。一則就是替某明星，或是某張片子大登廣告，吸引一般人的注意。二則它們可以吸引許多年輕美貌的女子，到好萊塢支代替那些公司當局們已經覺得厭倦的演員們。　　現在電影雜誌裏，受過份的宣傳的明星，第一位是葛雷泰嘉寳。差不多一本雜誌，没有她一叚新聞，或是一張相片，就好像是不完全是的。第二是梅蕙絲。對於她的宣傳方法，亦更是肉麻到萬份了。其餘的像約翰吉爾勃，因爲和嘉寳合演「克利斯丁娜的緣故，亦受了遠過所應得的宣傳。至於琪恩哈羅，珍尼蓋諾等，都是在長年宣傳之列的人物。當然這種宣傳文字和照相，和廣勂地是有連鎖關係的。聽說有兩家雜誌，因爲没有梅蕙絲新片子的廣告，她的照片，就此不登，並且在評論之中，亦絶口不提取她的名字。因此，我們可以說美的電影雜誌，大都全是好萊塢的宣傳工俱罷了。（未完）影片談評「紅寳石」評  凌鶴Ｔh（estory　of　"Bomday　Mai"）　　丨國泰丨　　和其他偵探片一樣，這裏也有一個離奇曲折的故事，故作驚人之筆，使人們耐着心情等待着殺人盜案之水落石出，而舒舒服服地走出戲院。自然，這便是娱樂。　　假使我們也承認這個故事的確編得不壞，那末，就得說這是在「羅馬快車」之外又有一個自始至終全發生在火車中的影片了，雖然，前者是社會劇，而這是偵探片。此外，一般的偵探片，殺人兇手多爲窮兇極惡的大盜，而這裏却使省長的秘書作爲兇手，這未嘗不是比較特别的地方。官長殺人，所謂「知法犯法」，換句話說，殺人者爲官，這的確是大膽的筆法。當然，劇作者要使官吏殺人，所以其官必貪，於是乎受賄畏罪便是他殺人的動機了。因此，假使說這一個戲也值得回味，那末，便使我們認識了官塲黑幕之可怕了。不過話得說回來，「紅寳石」到底不過是平凡的偵探片，詎被殺與誰爲殺人者，在作者都可以不加選擇，坂正就不過賣弄一點虛構的偵探學而已。難道說殺人者爲省長秘書但是最大的主題嗎？很顯明的並未如此。反之，正如上面所述，無非是離奇曲折的故事，以電影藝術作爲生産工具罷了。至於在十幾節火車中展開一個複雜的故事，自然是經過了嚴密的檯思，這未嘗不是值得稱讚之處。然而這始終是美國藝人在極力賣弄技巧而已。　　另一方面，在導演者聰明的手法中，也是很技巧的。雖無特别優長，而亦無不通或不够表現之處。每一個嫌疑犯出塲，都處理得好，而伏綫的暗示，亦甚可取。同時爲了要避免沉悶的空氣，間或使用着緊張的塲面，甚至於當作劇的高潮。如毒蛇自皮中爬出，霍雷在疾馳着的火車頂上爬行。這些，無疑的都是導演弄巧之處。此外也照例的穿揷了不少噱頭。　　至於愛德門羅的表演，不知怎麽的，總不容易討好，他不是賣力的從事沉着的表演，而是在賣弄文明戲味兒的小聰明。其他諸人，更無可述之處。「風流天子」雜話  素素　　「風流天子」一片，大上海映後，接着就在金城放映，風頭之健，無以復加。有人說：「這個片子的號召能力，當歸功說那三百六十五位后妃，並不是伊密爾詹寗氏，」是否實在，尚待考證。　　在英文說明上，寫着三百六十六位后妃。在對白中，又明明說着三百六十五位后妃，有人對於這件事情，非常懐疑。實在這個啞謎是容易打破的，因爲年年是三百六十五天。不過到了閏年，却有三百六十六天，於是風流天子的后妃，到了閏年，也不能不增加一位了。　、　、據說，當這部片子到滬的時候，影片商人，對於中文名稱，打算把它譯爲「阿房宫」三字。但是後來恐怕「阿房宫」三字不能通俗，才譯爲今名「風流天子」。實在照我看起來，「阿房宫」三字，多少要比較雅緻點，並且也未嘗不通俗，質之高明，以爲然否。（却酬）　　藝華公司新片「烈焰」一幕胡萍彭飛主演不日開映。滑稽鉅片「巧連環」光陸蘭心今日公映　　英國滑稽夫婦搭擋賈克赫爾勃，西施考德，自從現身「杏花天」以來，轟動影壇，滿載美譽。「杏花天」爲本埠蘭心大戲院開幕貢，盛極一時，海上影迷，多以一覩爲快。最近他倆偉大傑搆「巧連環」較之「杏花天」有過之無不及。表演出神入化，一舉一動，諧趣叢生。該片取影瑞士，瑞士爲世界名勝之區，且終年帶雪，幾幕大自然之美景，尤爲美觀。刦利卓别麟的近狀  福　大家都知道利用人們的好奇心，而增高自己的聲價的。葛萊泰嘉寳，凱絲玲海嬪等，都是個中的斵輪老手，但是却利卓别靈亦不讓於人。他直到於今，還晃　没有演過有聲片，但是他們却能够偶然的在無線廣播之中，略爲露一露他的罄欬，打動人的好奇心。現在他正在計劃著一張新片子，可是他對人，絶口不道那張新片子的内容。有人說，他要改變方針而拍有聲片子，但他旣不承認，又不否認，至於他的「燈籠袴子」，大皮靴，小手杖等等，是否放棄呢？還是保留呢？大家亦揣測不透。有人說他的小鬍子將要剃去了，但是誰知道？這是個怪人，他連自己的老婆，到底娶了没有，却不肯告訴人。不過大家都說保勒蒂哥達德在秘密的地方，實在是他的老婆了。麗琳哈蕙卽將脫離銀幕生活？  樹勛　　　　素以活潑窈窕著稱之紅影星麗琳哈蕙，自主演「龍翔鳳舞」「鳳求凰」等片後，聲譽雀起，極受美人之欣賞。頃閱某西報好萊塢通訊，據稱麗琳對銀燈生活，已表示倦意，决卽脫離影界，聞者均不勝婉惜云。據該西報稱，麗琳已飯嘗銀幕生活，頗覺乏味，亟思一享家庭生活樂趣。目下渠在好萊塢所住之華麗大厦，及炫目之攝影塲，已非渠所歡。渠所切盼者，乃一體貼入微之郎君，及活潑之小孩耳。　　此外麗琳近與狐狸公司之糾葛。亦是促成她退隱原因之一。聞麗琳對公司一方面强迫渠在某片說德法兩種語言，表示不滿，將訴諸法律云。　　據麗琳之至友云，麗琳現已屬意於威利非力，認爲理想丈夫。威利爲德國著名男星，前在德與麗琳合演影片頗多。聞麗琳現爲預備敎養將來愛情結晶品起見，已在别墅旁建一小兒樂園，伊求子心之切，於此可見。電影小說凱塞琳女皇（Ｓcarlet　Empress）（三）  素梅　　到了明天，宫裏大家急急忙忙地預備着育漢娜公主和蘇斐亞公主出門的行裝，因爲亞萊克賽公爵催促着要早日動身。從普魯士到莫斯科，一路的馬車雪車，要走七個禮拜之久，而俄國的女皇是朝朝夜夜，在等待着這新婦的蒞臨。奥古斯都親王，育漢娜公主，和蘇斐亞的許多姑母，大家一齊監督着僕役們工作着。育漢娜因爲期望太切了，心裏覺得忐忑不安起來。蘇斐亞的幾個姑母，亦覺得這個婚姻是無上的光榮，都露着興高彩烈的神氣。祇有奥古斯都親王一個人，愁思滿面的，一天一天的沉默起來。不久，動身的時候到了。蘇斐亞抱住了奥古斯都親王，她的心感覺到尖銳的刺痛，和他辭别。奥古斯都亦撫摸着她，給了她許多爲人之道的敎訓。他柔聲的說道：「蘇斐亞，你不久就要萬里長征。我或者永久和你不再相見······我要你切記我所敎訓你的話·····就是忠實不欺，做一個良妻，忠心於你的新國家·········對於下屬要仁慈，對於你的丈夫和在你之上的要順從······」他似不勝兒女之情，所以說話是斷斷續續的。最後他又鼓起了勇氣說道：「你要爲你光榮的前途而努力，不可自甘暴棄。」他說完了，將蘇斐亞緊抱在胸口温存著。蘇斐亞流著涙，看著她的父親道：「父親，我不願意離開你！」但是育漢娜的聲音，無情的一聲喊，生生將他們父女分散了，而這一位，未來的女沙皇，亦就此推推挽挽地被擁進車子裏去了。　蘇斐亞一路在車子裏，好似走着無窮無盡的長途，但是每轉一個彎，總要如悲如怨的回顧一下，好像自己知道此次遠行，是和故鄉遠别似的。這樣的一腔悲憤，就是她新生命的開始丨那新生命亦就將她原有的和婉仁慈的心，摧毁無遺，而將她化成了狠心的婦人丨一位要人謹愼服侍，時時懐懼的一個皇后。這七個星期的旅行，在蘇斐亞廻想之中，好似一塲惡夢。不久她的馬車換了雪撬，在一片皚白的冰天雪地之中走着，寒風刺骨，冷不可當，而她活潑可愛的心情，亦就隨之而變換了。一路上惟一可以使蘇斐亞的心，感覺到一些人間的温暖的，亦祇有少年公爵亞萊克賽的不時煦拂，而亞萊克賽對於蘇斐亞的愛慕，亦竟一天一天的滋長起來了。很巧的有一天，他們到了一家客店裏，僕役們已經陪伴着育漢娜公主到裏面去了，亞萊克賽在和蘇斐亞談話之間，竟將她抱在他的懐裏，蘇斐亞亦毫不抵抗的將香唇給他吻着，一回兒她將公爵推開了，開他道；「你爲什麽要這樣呢？」公爵道：「我的小公主呀，就是因爲我已經傾心於你了。「他說完了，就將鞭了交給了她說道「現在請你懲罰我的大不」敬吧！」（未完）

1934.03.09

Southern Route Army Awaits Orders for General Offensive in Bandit Areas 1

(Hong Kong) The First Column of the Southern Route Army has decided to first attack the Yudu bandit area. The First Division passed through Xinfeng and opened to An'yuan on the 8th. The Fourth Division has completely moved to Nankang and Ganzhou, awaiting orders. The Second Division has also moved to the northeast of Xinfeng. (Central News Agency Dispatch, 8th)

(Hong Kong) Huang Guangrui convened an air force conference on the 8th, assigning squadrons to provide cover for the various armies entering Gan to suppress bandits. (Special Dispatch, 8th)

Military Headquarters Strictly Orders Military Police to Maintain Military Discipline 2

(Nanjing) The Military Headquarters has established six points of attention for military police to maintain military discipline, ordering strict correction of local military personnel who do not abide by military discipline. (Central News Agency Dispatch, 8th)

Sun Dianying Shows No Sincere Intention to Leave the Army 3

Building Several Defense Lines in Ningxia

Fu Zhan Kui Has Yet to Meet Sun

Fu Zuoyi and Others Telegraph Sun, Urging His Final Awakening

If He Does Not Rein in at the Brink, There Will Only Be Military Confrontation

(Beiping) Despite the ceasefire and Fu Zhan Kui's arrival in Dengkou to meet with Sun, Sun shows no sincere intention to leave the army. The rumors of his stepping down are merely a tactic by Sun's side to ease tensions. Furthermore, the reports of Liu Yueting and Yang Hou's small units fleeing to Zhongwei and Liangzhou are completely inaccurate. (Dispatch, 8th)

(Beiping) A dispatch from Baotou states that Sun's army is facing supply shortages due to the sparse population west of Wuzizui and the Ningxia authorities' scorched-earth policy. An offensive is difficult, and the increasing threat from the advancing Jin-Sui armies in the rear has created a dilemma. Sun's forces have established four defense lines in Bulunnuo, Dengkou, and Shizuizi. Strong fortifications have been built in the Bulunnuo area, defended by more than two brigades. Three defense lines are being actively constructed in the Sanshenggong-Shizuizi area. Ma Hongkui telegraphed Fu Zuoyi, stating that Sun's army has launched several fierce attacks recently, all of which have failed. The traffic to western Baotou is difficult, and military rations and horse fodder must be purchased and transported from Baotou. The Beiping Military Branch sent a heavy-duty truck, escorted by Major Lin Fu, to Baotou yesterday for the Jin army's use. Fu appointed Zhao Jinbiao, a counselor from his department, as the station commander, requisitioning all vehicles in Jin province to facilitate military use. (Special Dispatch, 8th)

(Tianjin) A dispatch from Suiyuan states that although Sun has repeatedly declared his willingness to leave the army and downsize his troops as ordered, he has yet to take any clear action. Fu Zuoyi, Wang Jingguo, and Zhao Chengshou, seeing Sun's ambiguous attitude, jointly telegraphed Sun with a final warning, urging him to awaken and leave the army soon. They stated that if he does not rein in at the brink, there will only be a large-scale encirclement and suppression, leading to military confrontation. It is said that at the start of the war, the Jin-Sui armies planned to recapture Dengkou within seven days. (Special Dispatch, 8th)

(Beiping) Sun's army, which was left east of Linhe, has been defeated by the Jin-Sui armies, and the Jin-Sui troops are also advancing. (Special Dispatch, 8th)

(Beiping) Fu Zhan Kui telegraphed that he arrived in Sanshenggong from Linhe at noon on the 6th, but there has been no news of him meeting with Sun. (Special Dispatch, 8th)

(Beiping) A Guihua dispatch states that the troops led by Da Tong are heading to Baotou, continuing westward. The vanguard of the Jin army crossed the river near Balagai, where they will officially come into contact with Sun. After Fu's departure, Yuan Yiqing will serve as the security commander, maintaining the rear. The command headquarters has been established, and a military law group for wartime operations is being drafted. (Special Dispatch, 8th)

(Beiping) A dispatch from Lanzhou states that Sun Dianying is investigating Lu Fengnian's troops, who have arrived in the vicinity of Ning. Yue Ting Ding (missing characters) have set up four defense lines in eastern Ning to defend against attacks by the Jin-Sui armies. Yang Hucheng has been ordered to transfer Feng Qinzai's troops, stationed in Tongguan, to the Yanan and Yulin areas to prevent Sun's army from fleeing south. (Special Dispatch, 8th)

(Beiping) The Sun Dianying incident is still largely being resolved militarily. Fu Zhan Kui is currently stationed in Huangyang Mutou and has telegraphed Sun, requesting a meeting in Dengkou, but Sun has not responded, demonstrating his lack of sincere repentance. The Jin army has decided to advance immediately towards Dengkou. Lu Fengnian of Sun's forces sent a representative, Yu Muxing, to Beiping to meet He Yingqin, expressing sincerity and stating that he could urge Sun to leave the army, but hoping that his troops would be reorganized. A spokesperson for the military branch stated that the authorities' approach to Sun's troops remains unchanged: (1) Sun leaves the army; (2) The troops withdraw to their original defense area; (3) The troops are downsized according to the number recorded by the military branch. Yu will leave Beiping to report back within the day. (Special Dispatch, 8th)

(Xi'an) Yang Hucheng ordered Feng Qinzai's 42nd Division on the 6th to completely move to the Yanan area of northern Shaanxi. The Wu Brigade has already departed. Feng has ordered all units to depart and will personally go to northern Shaanxi to strengthen the military presence and prevent Sun's army from fleeing south. The defenses around Tongguan will be taken over by Tian Jingyi's brigade. (Central News Agency Dispatch, 7th)

(Beiping) A dispatch from Ningxia on the 7th stated that since the enemy army invaded Ningyuan, they have suffered heavy losses from our repeated attacks and have lost their fighting ability. They are currently being suppressed. The enemy troops are being tightly blocked and cannot escape. The rumors of Yang Hou and Liu Yueting fleeing to Zhongwei and Liangzhou are completely inaccurate. (Special Dispatch, 8th)

(Beiping) Although there has been much talk of peaceful solutions regarding the Sun Dianying problem recently, the hope of achieving them remains bleak. After arriving in Linhe, Fu Zhan Kui telegraphed Sun several times, requesting a meeting at a chosen location, but Sun has not responded in any way. Fu has had to temporarily stop at Huangyang Mutou, waiting for Sun's actions. According to general observations, Sun still shows no sign of awakening, and the so-called compliance with the order to leave the army is all false pretense. Fu's trip is simply to fulfill his friendship and make a final effort to mediate, hoping to ascertain whether Sun is truly sincere. The authorities here have consistently maintained a policy of both suppression and appeasement, and they will not become optimistic simply because Sun has expressed a desire to leave the army. Encirclement and suppression will not cease until Sun leaves the army and withdraws his troops to the designated area for downsizing. Fu Zuoyi, in particular, is deeply angered by Sun's previous expansion of military forces in western Suiyuan, disrupting the local area and hindering the proper administration of Sui politics. He advocates for a thorough solution to eliminate this threat to the Northwest. The Jin-Sui armies have been ordered to advance with all haste. Fu Zuoyi and Wang Jingguo are both in Baolin, directing military affairs. They will first recapture Sanshenggong within days and then advance towards Dengkou. Sun's troops are exhausted, and although they may want to resist stubbornly, it will be difficult. Lu Fengnian, a brigade commander under Sun, has sent a representative to Beiping to negotiate surrender, suggesting that Lu lead Sun's troops to join the Jin-Sui army and be reorganized. The prerequisite is Sun's departure from the army. The Jin-Sui army will follow the authorities' orders in this regard. It was rumored that the Military Branch commander would allow passage through Shaanxi and Gansu to enter Ning and help suppress Sun's army. According to a statement from Shang, there was indeed such a proposal a month ago, but the timing is still unclear. (Central News Agency Dispatch, 8th)

Shen Bao, Second Page

Current Affairs Commentary

The US Naval Expansion Plan and the Far East Problem 19

According to a foreign dispatch from the 7th, the naval expansion bill, passed by the US House of Representatives at the end of January, has been passed by a majority in the Senate. According to the US Constitution, if the President does not oppose the bill, it can take effect. Considering the current political situation in the United States, Roosevelt will certainly approve the bill, as the Democratic Party occupies an absolute majority in both the US Senate and House of Representatives, and Roosevelt himself is the leader of the Democratic Party. Reasonably, problems will not arise. However, if the President opposes the bill, according to the US Constitution, the President can only request the two houses to reconsider. If the two houses re-vote on the previous proposal, it will become law. Therefore, the passage of this naval expansion bill is virtually assured.

The bill stipulates that the United States will build 102 warships and 1,184 naval aircraft in the next seven years. Although the amount of increase is within the scope of the Washington Naval Treaty, its purpose is undoubtedly to address the Far East problem. Since the Democratic Party took office in the United States, its attitude towards Japan has been vague and unpredictable. When the Republican Party was in power, although it did not exert real pressure on Japan, Stimson repeatedly declared his disagreement to express the party's position. However, since Roosevelt took office, the United States first passed the Philippine independence bill after twelve years, implicitly indicating that it had no intention of contending for supremacy in the Far East. Secondly, it focused on the economic recovery of the country and did not ask about other matters. Even its recognition of Soviet Russia was justified by economic motives. Moreover, after recognizing Soviet Russia, it moved its fleet in the Pacific to the Atlantic. Virtually every action was intended to dispel Japan's suspicions and ease the war clouds in the Pacific.

Judging from the traditional foreign policy of the US Democratic Party, Roosevelt's actions seemed appropriate for the party. The Democratic Party's foreign policy was originally the Monroe Doctrine. The meaning of the Monroe Doctrine is twofold: First, domestic affairs come before foreign affairs; second, we do not offend others, and others do not offend us. Therefore, its foreign policy is more defensive than offensive, and its pursuit of foreign territories is also relatively passive. Therefore, after the Democratic Party's victory in the US general election last year, the Japanese were delighted, hoping that the party would adhere to the Monroe Doctrine and abandon its hegemony in the Far East. For a year, the US government has indeed no longer issued declarations similar to Stimson's on the Far East problem, and its actions have been aimed at dispelling Japan's suspicions. It is as if its foreign policy still adheres to the Monroe Doctrine of the past. However, from our point of view, the US Democratic Party's Far East policy is not that simple. Although the Monroe Doctrine is the traditional policy of the Democratic Party, if other countries endanger the interests of the United States, even according to the Monroe Doctrine, it is necessary to come forward to defend them. This can be proven by the facts. Therefore, the current Monroe Doctrine of the United States cannot be regarded as a policy of isolation. When President Wilson was in power, the Democratic Party and the Republican Party jointly advocated participation in the war without the slightest hesitation. Therefore, although the Democratic Party has expressed its intention to abandon the Philippines, it cannot be said that it will relax its hegemony in the Far East.

However, the US Democratic Party's policy is cautious and thorough, and it will only act after full preparation. Therefore, before preparations are complete, it will not make empty declarations or issue futile threats, and it will deliberately show people that it is not aggressive to reduce Japan's hostility. Therefore, its skill is better than Stimson's arrogant pronouncements. Observing the naval expansion bill passed by the two houses today, one can know a glimpse of its determination. The Washington Treaty will soon expire. After its expiration, Japan will greatly expand its navy to establish its position as the hegemonic power of East Asia. If the United States does not first strengthen its naval power within the limits permitted by the treaty, it will be difficult to restrain Japan at that time and lose its say on the Far East problem. Therefore, the passage of this US naval expansion bill is as important as its recognition of Soviet Russia, and it also indicates that it does not want to abandon its position in the Far East. It is seen that Japan's Hirota still wants to promote the independence of the Philippines and divide the hegemony of the Pacific Ocean between East and West to seek the friendship of Japan and the United States, showing that his efforts are in vain.

Easing Relations with Italy: German Deputy Prime Minister to Visit Rome 22

Negotiations with the Vatican

His arrival, neither early nor late, coincides with the visit of the Austrian and Hungarian Prime Ministers.

General speculation suggests the aim is to hinder the political alliance of the three countries.

Rome: According to today's news, German Deputy Prime Minister Franz von Papen will arrive in Rome on March 14th. This trip coincides with the visits of the Austrian and Hungarian Prime Ministers, which is particularly noteworthy. The mission of the Austrian and Hungarian Prime Ministers is to seek the establishment of an economic solution for the Danube countries. However, Deputy Prime Minister Papen's visit to Rome is reportedly aimed at reopening negotiations with the Vatican. Negotiations between Germany and the Roman Catholic Church broke down in February due to Dr. Alfred Rosenberg, subordinate to German Chancellor Adolf Hitler, authored a book titled "The Myth of the Twentieth Century." The Roman Catholic Church deemed it absurd, barbaric, wildly unrestrained, and contradictory to Christian doctrine and humanism, and subsequently banned it. This is the origin of the breakdown of negotiations. At the same time, the German National Socialist Party attempted to attract Catholic youth groups to join the Hitler Youth movement. Germany also arrested clergymen, accusing them of propagating political conspiracies. This is another reason for the strained relations between the Vatican and Germany. Papen's arrival in Rome is likely to ease this tense relationship. In addition, Papen likely has other purposes. According to some viewpoints, Papen will try to approach Italy, and if possible, will hinder the political alliance of Italy, Austria, and Hungary. This statement seems not without reason. The visit of the Austrian and Hungarian Prime Ministers to Italy has already aroused considerable suspicion in Germany, because the current balance of power, if shifted by this visit, is naturally not welcomed by Germany. With the Treaty of Trianon established, Hungary lost land, while the South Slav countries greatly benefited. Now Italy wants to revise the treaty, which is genuinely opposed by the South Slav countries. The result of the Italian, Austrian, and Hungarian conference may lead to Italy supporting the restoration of the Austro-Hungarian Empire, which is also feared by Germany. If Italy agrees to be the backer of Austria-Hungary, the demand for the restoration of defense projects on the Austro-Hungarian border will inevitably follow. The Austrian and Hungarian Prime Ministers will stay in Rome for three days. Will they meet with Papen at that time? It is impossible to predict, but there is no indication of such a meeting currently. Papen may intend to seek a friendly solution with Austrian Prime Minister Dollfuss, but observers of the European situation believe that this is unlikely to happen. (Reuters dispatch, 7th)

Vienna: It is rumored that Deputy Prime Minister Papen will soon travel to Rome, and his arrival in Rome will coincide with the meeting of the Austrian, Italian, and Hungarian Prime Ministers in Rome. However, informed sources this morning could not verify this rumor, and said that the Austrian government had not contacted diplomatic channels regarding Papen's trip to Rome. Therefore, even if Papen goes to Rome, Austrian Prime Minister Dollfuss will not negotiate with Papen in Rome. (Havas dispatch, 8th)

Italy-Austria-Hungary Conference: Economic and Commercial Matters Take Precedence Over Politics 23

Vienna: The Ministry of Foreign Affairs announced that Prime Minister Dollfuss will depart for Rome on the 13th of this month to hold a meeting with Italian Prime Minister Mussolini and Hungarian Prime Minister Gömbös. Director-General Schüller of the Department of Foreign Trade Agreements has already gone to Rome to contact Italian business personnel to prepare for the meeting of the three Prime Ministers in Italy, Austria, and Hungary at the technical level. Informed sources here firmly stated that the purpose of this meeting is to promote economic relations between the three countries, and particular attention will be paid to expanding business relations between Austria and Hungary. (Havas dispatch, 7th)

France Courts Belgium 24

Foreign Minister's Visit to Brussels on Monday

Contains Important Political Significance

Unwavering Attitude on Disarmament

Reply to England to be Sent Out Within Days

"Le Petit Parisien" Reveals Five Points of Demands

(Paris) French Foreign Minister Barthou will visit Brussels next Monday for special reasons. (Guomin News Agency dispatch, 8th)

(Paris) Following Belgian Prime Minister de Broqueville's speech in parliament yesterday, in which he supported the principle of German arms equality, French public opinion felt uneasy. Many newspapers said that de Broqueville's remarks did not represent the public opinion of the Belgian people. Furthermore, French Foreign Minister Barthou will soon visit Brussels. Although the government announced that this trip is merely Barthou's personal courtesy to Belgian Foreign Minister Hymans, considering the current diplomatic situation, there are quite a few political elements involved. Perhaps the purpose of Barthou's trip is to prevent Belgium from changing its direction on the issue of disarmament. Furthermore, there is another matter for reference: "Le Petit Parisien" published another editorial today, reiterating France's unwavering attitude on armaments, stating that France's reply to the British memorandum has been prepared and can be sent out within days, and there is still room for negotiation in the future. However, France has put forward several key points, which seem to no longer need to be discussed.

Five Demands 25

(1) The increase of German armaments must not occur without the prior unanimous consent of all countries. (2) The increase of German armaments and the reduction of France's defense capabilities cannot occur simultaneously, as this would create a double layer of danger. (3) In addition to formal armies, no paramilitary organizations may exist. (4) All strength and armament reports should have universal and reliable methods of monitoring. (5) There must be guarantees as to how common disarmament methods will be implemented in the future.

"Le Petit Parisien" claims that the Allied countries have already agreed with France regarding the fifth point, but this statement is indeed very unbelievable. (Guomin News Agency dispatch, 8th)

Belgian Prime Minister and Foreign Minister's Declaration on Disarmament Opposed by Senate 26

Belgian Policy Lies in Preventing Aggression from Neighbors

German Rearmament Endangers Peace

Brussels: Foreign Minister Hymans stated in the Senate today regarding the issue of disarmament that, judging from the diplomatic exchange of documents, it can be seen that although countries have the same views on some points regarding the issue of disarmament, there are still significant differences of opinion. The greatest difficulty lies in the issue of the German militarization of the police and military groups outside the formal army. There is a danger of widespread rearmament in Germany, which we should be wary of. However, since the current international situation does not allow for the use of force to resolve disputes, we can only consider concrete solutions and establish an international disarmament treaty to restrict it. If France, Britain, and Italy can reach a compromise, then this treaty should be effective. Hymans also said that Belgium attaches great importance to the Rhine Agreement within the Locarno Treaty, which guarantees the borders of Belgium. He concluded that Belgium is determined to make people respect its territory. (Havas dispatch, 7th)

Brussels: The political and press circles here do not approve of the speeches made by Prime Minister de Broqueville and the Foreign Minister in the Senate on the issue of disarmament. The attitude of disapproval in the Senate today is even stronger than yesterday. Senator Serruys, Chairman of the Senate Foreign Affairs Committee, representing the opinions of most senators, said that Belgian policy lies in preventing dangerous neighbors from rearming. (Havas dispatch, 7th)

Wartime Industrial Mobilization

Air Defense Arrangements

Pétain Attends Senate Army Committee to Explain

(Paris) The Senate Army Committee held a meeting, and the Finance, Navy, Aviation, and Foreign Affairs committees also sent members to listen. Army Minister General Pétain made detailed explanations on the following points:

(1) The defensive fortifications on the northwest and southeast borders of France. (2) The general organizational status of the high command of the army, navy, and air force. England Increases Army Budget 30

Total Amount of £45 Million

Improving Coastal Defenses

Mechanizing Military Equipment

Two Heavy Artillery Battalions Transferred to Singapore

(London) The 1934 British Army budget, announced today by War Minister Hailsham, totals £45,373,000, an increase of £1,650,000 over last year's budget. The army has a total of 149,500 personnel, an increase of 800 from last year. The War Minister stated in his statement that this budget is £330,000 less than the budget in 1931. Therefore, the increased amount is still lower than the special reductions made to respond to the panic in 1932. The increased funds in this budget will be used to (1) improve coastal and other defenses, (2) continue the mechanization process, (3) construct appropriate storage facilities, (4) improve barracks, and (5) increase training facilities. (Reuters dispatch, 8th)

(London) The British government plans to transfer two heavy artillery battalions to Singapore to increase defenses. (Guomin News Agency dispatch, 7th)

Vinson Act Passed by Congress: US Navy Secretary Expresses Gratitude 31

Creating a Perfect Navy

Responding to Future Events

(Washington) US Navy Secretary Swanson expressed his deep gratitude today for the House of Representatives' passage of the Vinson-Trammell Act. This act will bring the strength of the United States Navy to the limits stipulated by the Naval Conference Treaty. Swanson stated today during his meeting with reporters that the United States has decided to create a perfect navy sufficient to respond to events. Georgia Congressman Vinson declared that the United States is not responsible for the world's arms race situation, but since the United States is one of the world's countries, it cannot help but pay attention when formulating national policies. (Guomin News Agency dispatch, 7th)

Roosevelt Sets Date for Pacific Tour in Mid-April 32

Hopes for Early Passage of Budget and Tax Treaty Bills by Congress

Plans to Return Airmail to Private Management

(Washington) President Roosevelt suggested to the Post Office Committees of both houses of Congress that, as soon as possible, airmail affairs should be entrusted to private companies, and negotiations should be started with various companies to establish new contracts. In addition, the President wants Congress to adjourn on April 15th, and will ask Congress to fully discuss the following two matters to promote the economic recovery program: (1) the budget bill, (2) the bill requesting presidential authority on tariff issues. Regarding this point, he hopes to obtain victory. The President also wants to make the Economic Recovery Administration a permanent agency. The agency has the power to refuse to issue sales licenses to industrialists who do not comply with the recovery industry regulations to sanction them. This power will expire at the end of June this year, and the agency has not used it so far. The President now plans to expand this power. It is generally believed that the President will soon exercise this power, but the first step is only to explain the implementation of industry regulations. After Congress adjourns, Roosevelt will travel to the Pacific via the Panama Canal for inspection. (In January of this year, Roosevelt declared that if Congress could adjourn early, he would travel to Hawaii via the Virgin Islands and Puerto Rico to inspect the Pacific). (Havas dispatch, 7th)

Mrs. Roosevelt Wanders in the West Indies 33

Unaccustomed to Staying Deep in the White House; Enjoys Traveling

Assisting the President in Implementing the New Deal

St. Thomas Island: Mrs. Roosevelt came to visit the West Indies and arrived here today, to great acclaim. She was accompanied by four female reporters and two photographers. Mrs. Roosevelt relayed to those welcoming her President Roosevelt's respect for the people of the island. After a short rest, she went out to enjoy the scenery and then went to the government office to participate in a reception. In the past, many First Ladies have stayed deep in the White House, managing household affairs, but Mrs. Roosevelt is not like that. Since her husband assumed the presidency, she has traveled over 40,000 miles and given about 70 speeches, and she has also paid close attention to the implementation of the New Deal. St. Thomas Island is one of the West Indies islands, purchased by the United States from Denmark in 1917, with a population of about 10,000. (Reuters dispatch, 7th)

Austrian Restoration Movement 34

Royalists Gather in the Capital

Key Figures Return to the Country to Participate

Vienna: Although officialdom and various parties here have repeatedly denied news about the Royalist Party's meeting, the action of key figures from the Royalist Party of Austria and Hungary gathering in Vienna has been widely known since this Wednesday, and it is known that they have formally met repeatedly to discuss the restoration of the Habsburg monarchy. The figures gathered include former Ambassador to the United States Count Széchényi, Count Károlyi, and Duke Hohenberg, all of whom arrived here on Tuesday. When the main figures of the Royalist Parties of the two countries formally met on Wednesday, Austrian Defense Minister Hardegg (a well-known and enthusiastic Royalist) hosted a banquet for key Imperialist figures from Hungary at his residence. Also, according to Mr. Wezsnera, speaking to representatives of the press, as soon as the authorities formally announce the cancellation of Archduke Otto's exile order, Archduke Otto will return to Vienna and will be the most promising to regain the throne. (Guomin News Agency dispatch, 8th)

(London) British-French commercial negotiations are scheduled to begin on March 14th at the Department of Commerce. French Commerce Minister Lamoureux and several experts arrived in London at the beginning of this week to prepare for the meeting. British Have New Proposals Regarding British-Japanese Cotton Industry Negotiations 36

Main Claims Remain Unchanged

(London) England's answer regarding opening up the situation was sent to the Japanese delegation at 10 p.m. on the 7th. The contents briefly explain the claims from the beginning, and change their form of expression, but there is no change to the main points of the claims. The Japanese delegation is very dissatisfied. They are currently discussing how to deal with it. The fifth meeting between Britain and Japan is scheduled to be held on the 15th. (Japanese Union News dispatch, 7th)

(London) The British side delivered a new memorandum yesterday on the 7th. There is no change to the contents from what has been claimed. The third-country market, which the Japanese representatives oppose, is still under discussion. However, the proposal is changed in form, so the Japanese representatives naturally reject it. However, at the hope of Ambassador Matsudaira, methods of handling the situation are currently being discussed. However, because this matter is of great importance, no decision had been made by 1:00 a.m. on the 8th. The representatives are continuing to consult, and their attitude is extremely cautious. (Allied Press dispatch, 8th)

(London) It is certain that the main reason why the British abandoned their initial tough attitude and avoided a rupture to produce a compromise plan is that, at the British Cabinet meeting on the afternoon of the 7th, most cabinet members were concerned about the breakdown of the meeting and hoped that Commerce Minister Runciman would seek a mitigation strategy. The Commerce Minister also wished to retain the formal addition of the government as a last resort. Therefore, after repeated discussions, a strategy of loosely changing the topic was used. Regardless of the surface reasons for the British side, it is known that this change in attitude is because it is known that competition in the world market would be unfavorable to Britain if there was no coordination with Japan. Therefore, how Britain is striving to make the meeting a success can be seen from this. (Electric Communications dispatch, 8th)

(London) On the evening of the 7th, Ambassador Matsudaira to England went to the British Department of Commerce to sincerely discuss the British-Japanese consultation with Minister Runciman. As a result, both sides were willing to avoid a breakdown and aim for a satisfactory outcome. Also, at the consultation on the 8th, the Japanese representatives stated that they would consult their home country regarding the British proposal and respond at the meeting on the 14th. (Electric Communications dispatch, 8th)

Japanese House of Representatives Discusses Communist Issue 40

Hirota Announces Strict Crackdown

(Tokyo) Because of discussions about the problem of revising the Peace Preservation Law and the Third International issue, the House of Representatives special assembly was held on the 7th to discuss the two issues. It is said that the contents are as follows:

Miyako, Chairman of the Seiyukai Committee, asked:

How much funds does the Soviet Union supply to the Communist Party movement within Japan?

Foreign Minister Hirota replied:

This problem is not clear in Russia.

Takami of the Seiyukai asked:

Is there any negotiation started with the Russian side by the Foreign Minister about the treaty between Japan and the Soviet Union banning propaganda of communism?

Foreign Minister Hirota replied:

Japan needs to seriously crack down on Russians propagating communism within the country, and the "Manchukuo," which is related to Japan, also needs to find ways to expel the Communist Party.

Kōichi Sekō of the Seiyukai asked:

Are there any cases of Japanese diplomats stationed in Soviet Russia becoming red, and do any members of the Soviet Union's embassy in Japan have any instances of spreading the communist agenda?

Foreign Minister Hirota replied:

Inspecting the actual situation in Soviet Russia will give rise to anti-communist views.

Yoshiro Matsutani of the Kokumin Domei asked:

How many Japanese people are Communist Party members in Russia?

Foreign Minister Hirota replied:

There are dozens in total, divided into four factions, fighting each other. (National League dispatch, 8th)

Revolutionary Tide in Spain 41

Martial Law Declared Nationwide

Laborers Establish Unified Front

General Strike Begins in Various Industries

Madrid: The long-simmering revolutionary tide in Spain has suddenly surged again. The government declared martial law nationwide today. Earlier, the Interior Minister announced in Congress that the government did not need to declare martial law, but ten minutes later, the government issued an order declaring martial law. The strike tide initiated by the opposition to the government has worsened, with 100,000 workers currently on strike, which has further deteriorated the situation. The martial law order was announced at 1:10 p.m., and effective measures were taken at the same time to prevent the outbreak of a revolution. However, a more violent strike movement based on the revolutionary plan is being organized. The Lerroux government may soon collapse, as Prime Minister Lerroux is only supported by the right-wing party and the royalist party, and the power of these two parties is no longer sufficient to maintain it. Since the elections last November, there has been a conspiracy for a revolution, with the first step being to unite the Socialist Party, the Communist Party, and syndicalist groups to form a battle line. The situation became more serious after industrialists and employers announced wage cuts, leading to revolutionary tides and strike actions. Since the establishment of the so-called "Labor Front," the people's support for the government has decreased. The revolutionary plan has been well-prepared by the organizers and has focused on inciting the military and smuggling military equipment for the revolution. (Reuters dispatch, 7th)

Gold Turns into Cement 42

Major Theft Occurs in South Africa

US Treasury Department's Displayed Gold Coins Also Go Missing

(London) A box of gold transported from South Africa, containing 930 ounces of gold, worth £6,000, had complete seals on the box when it was unloaded in Southampton. Upon opening it, the gold in the box had turned into 930 ounces of cement. Judging from the situation, this shocking theft occurred in South Africa. At the same time, a theft unprecedented in history occurred in the display cabinet of the US Treasury Department in Washington. The cabinet was placed at the entrance of the Treasury Department and displayed gold coins worth £15 and some fake gold bars. This morning, all the displayed items were missing. If the gold bars were real, they would be worth 30,000 US Dollars. Treasury Department personnel found this very strange, as guards were on duty at the entrance when the Treasury Department doors were open. (Reuters dispatch, 7th)

Swedish Prince Lowers His Dignity 43

Formally Marries a German Businesswoman

(London) A Swedish prince and the daughter of a German businessman, who had appeared on screen, were married here this morning. Many curious people from London went to the Kensington registry office to watch the wedding, which was very simple. Members of the Swedish royal family had strongly advised the prince not to marry the businesswoman, but the prince did not budge and prepared a statement renouncing his royal rights. Several members of the Swedish royal family have previously renounced their rights due to marrying commoners. (Reuters dispatch, 8th)

Stable Currency: Britain and the United States Reach Tentative Understanding

U.S. Financial Circles Disbelieve Rumors

(New York) There are rumors in London that an informal understanding has been reached between London and New York to stabilize British and American currencies. These rumors are not believed by New York financial circles. However, the speculation may have originated from the visit of Chicago economic expert Professor Fan Yinna to England, as many view Professor Fan's trip to London as a prelude to accepting a senior position at the U.S. Treasury Department. However, bankers believe that under the current circumstances, there is no need to make efforts to stabilize British and American currencies. At the same time, responsible parties in London do not attach importance to the revival of such rumors. However, prominent British economist Stanford gave a speech in the Danish capital on March 7, stating that general public opinion is gradually advocating the restoration of the gold standard at the appropriate time and under the appropriate conditions. (Reuters, 8th)

(London) In mid-February, several non-governmental representatives, apparently with the permission of their respective governments, signed a secret contract to stabilize the pound and the dollar. This news has been confirmed today by a senior official. It is also heard that the economic expert Wenna, who recently visited London, presided over the establishment of this agreement. Although the contents of the agreement remain secret, the recent exchange rate between the pound and the dollar has hindered the participation of France and other gold standard countries. The United Kingdom may refuse to enter into a formal agreement, and London is also unwilling to conclude an agreement to stabilize currency with the United States, as this move may damage Anglo-French friendship. Since the devaluation of the dollar, commercial competition from the United States has intensified, so it remains doubtful whether the United Kingdom will agree to the permanent stabilization of the recent exchange rate. (National Telegram, 8th)

International Business Telegram

丨Special Commercial News Telegram from Reuters on March 8th丨

Gold and Silver

London Gold Price: Today's London gold price is 136 shillings and pence, down 2 pence from yesterday.

London Silver Price: Today's London silver price spot is 20 pence and 4375, futures is 20 pence and 5625. Spot up 0.0625, futures up 125. The United States and India bought, China sold.

New York Silver Price: The trend is bullish, and sentiment is quite good. Trading was not active in the morning. Traders are closely watching the situation in other markets. Forward openings are up 21 to 45 points compared to yesterday's close.

Bombay Silver Price: Today's Bombay silver market closed steadily. The spot price is 55 rupees and 9 annas, down 1 anna from yesterday.

Exchange Rate

British-American Exchange: The London foreign exchange market is calm. The opening British-American exchange rate is 5 yuan and 8 points 625, the same as yesterday's British-American exchange closing price. There was little change in the morning. The afternoon price at 2 p.m. was 5 yuan and 8 points 1875, down 4375 from the opening.

British-French Exchange: The opening was 77 francs, 55, the same as yesterday's close. At 1 p.m., it rose by 3 points to 77 francs 28, and remained unchanged until [time].

British-American Exchange Rate: At 2 p.m. today, the London exchange rate for New York was 5 yuan and 8 points 1875 U.S. dollars for one British pound. One U.S. dollar equaled 3 shillings and 11 pence 227 British gold.

U.S.-British Exchange Rate: New York's exchange rate for British pounds closed at 5.08625 on the previous day, opened at 5.0825 today, second board 5.0825, third board 5.0375, fourth board 5.8375, fifth board 5.08375.

U.S.-French Exchange Rate: The opening was 6.58, down 125 from yesterday's close.

Cotton and Wheat

New York Cotton: The opening was slightly up, due to slight purchases by brokers, bankers, and the Far East. Cotton prices continued to rise, due to good Liverpool telegrams and the hope that the Penhaid cotton production proposal will be submitted to the House of Commons today.

Bombay Cotton: The cotton market initially rose due to speculative buying to cover shorts, and then fell due to profit-taking. The four-five month term price for white Roche cotton was 201 rupees 75, up 1 rupee.

Liverpool Cotton: The May term fell by three points from yesterday to 6.25.

Liverpool Wheat: The market situation this morning remained loose. May term 4 shillings 4 pence, down half a penny.

Rubber

London: This afternoon, the London rubber market situation was looser, due to fewer buyers. The transaction price for the April-June term was 5 pence 32/3, down 32/3 from yesterday.

New York: The rubber market situation is calm and stable, expressing sympathy for London. Traders are now awaiting new news on rubber restrictions.

Metals

London: The tin price on today's metal exchange rose by 1 pound 6 shillings and 3 pence, reaching a price of 231 pounds per ton, the highest price since 1928.

Securities

New York: Today's securities market opened mixed, but eventually returned to calm, with slight anxiety, but confidence remained stable. It is difficult to grasp the recent situation going forward, due to labor unrest in the automotive industry and the development of recovery regulations. (2) Situation During the Review of Clothing

Details of Xu Minghong's Arrest and Execution

Disguised from Longyan to Dapu

The 19th Route Army Was Misled by Xu

Xiamen Correspondence: Xu Minghong, the former secretary of the 19th Route Army, was a major figure in the Fujian Rebellion, serving as the Deputy Director of the General Political Department of the so-called People's Government Military Commission and the Governor of Longting Province. After the outbreak of the war, Xu went from Fuzhou to Zhangzhou, presiding over the rear. When the 19th Route Army retreated to Quanzhou and the Central Army's 3rd Division landed on Songyu Island to attack Zhangzhou, Xu led Zhou Lixing and the Political Security Division to Longyan. When Cai Tingkai left Fujian, it was rumored that Xu led the Political Security Division to Tingzhou to join the Communist Party. In fact, Xu was still near Longyan. It was not until February 19th that he disguised himself and fled from Longyan to Dapu County, staying at the Tongtian Hotel. He was discovered by the local Guangdong Army, who sent police to arrest him. Xu was disguised as a soldier, with long strips of adhesive plaster on his forehead, wearing tea-colored glasses. He was taken to the Dapu County Government. The county magistrate reported to Huang Renhuan, the commander of the Independent 1st Division. Huang then acted upon Chen Jitang's telegram, stating that Xu had betrayed the party and the country, caused chaos, and harmed the people, and ordered him to be executed on the spot. On the morning of February 25th, he was taken from the prison to Dasha Dam and shot. Xu was quite composed. At the time of his death, he still had 300 yuan in cash. Xu gave 100 yuan to the prison officer, instructing him to buy a coffin for burial, and the remaining 200 yuan was to be sent to his elderly father. Xu was from Fengshun County, Guangdong Province, and was 39 years old. He was a student at Peking University and a former student of Liang Shuming. Before the Northern Expedition of the Party Army, Xu went to Guangdong through Liang Shuming's introduction, joining the political department of Chen Mingshu's division in the 4th Army as director. After the Northern Expedition, he joined the Communist Party in Wuhan. During the split between Ning and Hankou, Xu, as the director of the political department of the 12th Army, shouted "Down with Chen Mingshu." Because of this, Chen and Xu did not get along. When Ning and Hankou reunited, Zhang Fakui's unit, led by Ye Ting, rebelled from Nanchang and returned to Guangdong. At that time, Xu also left Hankou and served as a teacher in a certain middle school in Guangdong. Later, when the Communist Party rioted in Guangzhou, Xu was imprisoned by Li Jishen on suspicion. He was released on bail through Liang Shuming's telegram. After the 17th year of the Republic, Xu became close to Deng Yanda. Xu and Cai Tingkai were very close during his time in the 11th Army. In the following years, due to his old feud with Chen Mingshu, he did not join the 19th Route Army. After the Songhu War, the 19th Route Army was transferred to Fujian, and Cai then summoned Xu to Fujian, appointing him as the secretary-general of the 19th Route Army Headquarters. Xu specialized in handling post-war affairs in western Fujian, trying to implement his doctrine. The Communist Party laughed at him for not being thorough. In the 19th Route Army, Xu did not get along with the old-fashioned generals Huang Qiang, Mao Weishou, and others. Only Cai deeply trusted him. Shen Guanghan and Qu Shounian were also close to Xu. The Fujian Rebellion was the result of Cai's belief in Xu's words and his decision to launch the rebellion. Since Chen Mingshu had already come to Fujian, Cai mediated and Chen and Xu resolved their previous feud. After the failure, the generals of the 19th Route Army blamed Cai for lightly believing Xu's words and acting rashly. In Xu's last words, he expressed regret to his comrades in the 19th Route Army, knowing that he himself was the key to the success or failure of the 19th Route Army. However, it is a pity that Cai's relationship with Xu led to such a result for the 19th Route Army. (March 5th)

International Women's Day: Shanghai Women's Circles Held a Joint Celebration Yesterday. Both Mr. and Mrs. Cai Yuanpei Gave Speeches. Various Manufacturers Distributed Gifts on Site.

Yesterday was the 38th International Women's Day. The Shanghai Women's National Goods Movement Committee held a joint celebration of International Women's Day by the Shanghai women's community at the Lake Society Auditorium on Beijing Road at 2 p.m. yesterday. Many ladies participated. Cai Yuanpei, president of the Academia Sinica, and others gave sincere speeches. There were games, and various domestic goods manufacturers distributed gifts on site, making for a lively occasion. The details are recorded below.

Enthusiastic Participation from All Sectors

Yesterday, attendees included Cai Yuanpei, Wang Xiaolai, Pan Yangyao, Du Chongyuan, Xi Guansheng, as well as Pan Tang Guanyu, Cai Zhoujun, Lin Kecong, Yang Minghui, Wu Binghai, Huang Bingpei, Chen Guanggen, Lu Lihua from the women's community, and more than a thousand guests from all walks of life.

Photography of the Women's Community Joint Celebration (Photographed by Xu Tianzhang)

Report from the Presidium

After the ritual formalities, Mrs. Cai Yuanpei, Zhou Jun, from the presidium, first gave a report, saying, "We are in the Year of National Goods for Women, and today is International Women's Day. Looking back on the past, we have endless thoughts. Let's take clothing as an example. Fifty or sixty years ago, women stayed at home, and clothing was simple and mostly domestic goods. Twenty years ago, it was different. Recently, compared to the past, it is even more different. Women's clothing is increasingly seeking novelty, so there are endless changes, and the demand for raw materials is also increasing. Because domestic goods cannot satisfy people's desires, sales have plummeted, and the annual cash outflow to foreign countries is even more alarming. Today, women demand equality. The so-called equality should have full knowledge and full ability to serve society. For example, we should also strive to promote domestic goods to save the country from poverty and weakness and not lag behind others."

Then, Pan Tang Guanyu reported, saying, "Because the national goods movement in the past did not achieve significant results, the word 'women' is added to the Year of National Goods this year. Our women's community is not short of knowledgeable people, so we should promote domestic goods with sincere patriotism so that domestic goods can be sold well in the country. Furthermore, manufacturers should strive to improve the quality and quantity of their products to satisfy buyers. Then, the results will be even more significant."

Finally, Lin Kecong reported, saying, "Twenty-five years ago today, women's leaders in the United States, seeing the oppression of women, came out to protest and seek women's liberation. Although there is a so-called slogan of equality between men and women in our country, there are still many oppressed women in rural areas and factories. The biggest reason is economic oppression. On this bright and splendid March 8th, we should strive for the liberation of women and the entire nation. To seek liberation, we should break the economic oppression of imperialism. The way to do this is to promote domestic goods. From now on, we should work hard and do it practically. Then, the annual outflow of tens of millions of cash will be saved one day, and the sales of domestic goods will be prosperous."

Speeches from Guests from All Sectors

After the report, Cai Yuanpei, President of the Academia Sinica, gave a speech, saying, "I am very honored to participate in the National Goods Joint Celebration of the women's community today. I am especially pleased to see the grand occasion of today's meeting. However, when we examine the past customs import and export records, we are very saddened. Last year's trade deficit reached 700 million yuan. The reasons are: (1) Foreign countries use mechanized production, while China mostly uses manual manufacturing. Therefore, foreign products are more and better than our country's. (2) Foreign goods are cheaper because of the large production volume. Compared with foreign countries, our country's productivity is far behind. Therefore, in the future, we should increase productivity and make goods of good quality and low price. Those in power should supervise from the side, and people from all walks of life should encourage it. I believe there will be good results."

Then, Pan Yangyao gave a speech, saying, "Chinese people often like to be cheap. In the past, foreign goods, especially Japanese goods, were cheaper than domestic goods, so Chinese people have a habit of buying foreign goods. Every year, cash outflows cause the country and people to become poorer and weaker. In the future, we should develop the habit of buying and using domestic goods as a glory and buying and using foreign goods as a shame. Then, the sales of domestic goods can be revived. The women's community has the authority to buy sundries, so if the women's community is determined to buy domestic goods, the future of domestic goods will be bright."

Huang Renzhi gave a speech, saying, "The times are constantly changing. At first, people often took pride in opening Beijing goods stores, then changed to opening foreign goods stores. Recently, domestic goods companies have become increasingly developed, so in the future, people will take pride in opening domestic goods companies. Even the largest stores in China, such as Sincere and Wing On, will use domestic goods as a gimmick in the future. This shows a kind of change in the mentality of Chinese people regarding the purchase of goods."

There were also speeches from Wang Xiaolai, Lu Lihua, Fan Zhiping, and others. The long speeches are omitted.

Various Entertainment Programs

Lawsuit for Rent Increase Fails, Landlord Orders Tenants to Move Out. Industry & General Company in Litigation with Tenants. Trial Concluded Yesterday, Judgment Scheduled in Ten Days.

The houses in Shoupin Lane near Huade Road and Tilanqiao were originally the property of the former Italian Bank. In 1930, the rent was increased, with monthly rents of 22 yuan per room for city houses, 18 yuan for single-family residences, and 40 yuan for double-family residences. At that time, a contract was signed between the landlord and tenants, stating that neither party could increase or decrease the rent until the end of 1933. After the end of 1933, any increase or decrease would require negotiation between the landlord and tenants. However, soon after, the Italian Bank sold the property to the British Industry & General Company, which entrusted Gao Yi Public House to manage the rent. A rent increase dispute occurred last spring, and a lawsuit was filed in the court. The tenants presented the contract signed with the Italian Bank in the past to resist the landlord's request. The court also recognized the validity of the contract, which did not disappear due to the change of ownership, and rejected the landlord's request.

However, on November 20th last winter, Industry & General Company notified all 150 tenant households that the rent would be increased by 29 yuan per room for city houses, totaling 50 yuan, 13 yuan per month for single-family residences, totaling 31 yuan, and 33 yuan for double-family residences, totaling 73 yuan. The tenants replied to the landlord, stating that the market was sluggish and the previous contract should be maintained, and requested that the landlord withdraw the order. However, the landlord refused to accept the tenants' claims and further issued a notice stating that if they did not agree to the rent increase, they could move out. The negotiations between the two parties gradually became tense.

On January 10th this year, the landlord directly issued eviction orders, limiting the tenants to move out on January 20th. Because the tenants refused, they filed a mediation request with the First Special District Local Court, but it was unsuccessful. Therefore, they filed a lawsuit against more than 150 tenants to terminate the lease and request a judgment to return the houses. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Qiao Wanxuan held a hearing. The defendant hired lawyer Yuan Yang'an to defend them, while the plaintiff was represented by lawyer Lu Xingyuan, who stated the intent of the lawsuit and said that the plaintiff only requested that the defendants return the houses and was willing to waive the rent owed for January.

Lawyer Yuan then pointed out the inappropriateness of the plaintiff's disregard for the previous contract and failure to increase the rent, and stated that the plaintiff's lawsuit was actually due to the failure to increase the rent and force relocation. However, according to the customs of this city, tenants should not be asked to move unless the house has been renovated or the tenant owes three months' rent. The tenants in this case do not owe rent. The plaintiff said that the rent was owed for one month, but the plaintiff did not collect it, and it was not a renovation. How can the tenants be asked to move? Therefore, the plaintiff's lawsuit has no basis and should be rejected.

The plaintiff's lawyer then rose to argue that the landlord was also seeking profit. Now, the land price in that area has increased, and the landlord's expenses have increased, so they had to increase the rent to compensate. They then submitted a statement of income and expenses to the court for reference. However, the defendant also submitted a form for the court's reference. Judge Qiao then adjourned the hearing and scheduled the judgment for the 10th of this month.

Police Gathered at Jing'an Villa; Guangdong Native Xu Guangyou Arrested. Had Defrauded More Than 20,000 Yuan in Kobe. Years of Pursuit Ended with Arrest.

According to the Dagong News Agency, the Japanese police team from the Japanese Consulate General's Office, together with many Chinese and Western detectives from the Jing'an Temple Road Police Station, rushed to No. 1 Jing'an Villa on Jing'an Temple Road on the morning of the 7th (yesterday) at around 6 a.m. They arrested Xu Guangyou, also known as Lin Jieshen, from Xiangshan County, Guangdong Province, and sent him to the Consulate General's Office for interrogation. The Dagong News Agency reporter learned that Xu Guangyou, who worked in the accounting department of the Kyomachi Trading Company in Kobe, Japan, three years ago, had defrauded more than 24,000 yuan in cash using fraudulent means. The details are as follows:

Defrauded a Large Sum of Money

Xu Guangyou, a native of Xiangshan County, Guangdong Province, 34 years old, was an employee in the accounting department of the Kyomachi Trading Company in Kobe, Japan. In December 1931, he used fraudulent means to forge signed checks and defrauded 4,450 yuan from the Kobe, Hong Kong, and Shanghai Banking Corporation branches. On December 31st of the same month, he used the same method to defraud more than 3,640 taels of silver from the Kobe and Hong Kong banks and 2,300 yuan from the Yokohama Specie Bank. After several fraudulent operations, he defrauded a total of more than 24,000 yuan in cash.

Fled to Shanghai

After defrauding a large sum of money, Xu Guangyou, fearing that the matter would be exposed after a long time, took his Japanese wife, Ms. Shioka, and packed his belongings and fled to Hong Kong on a British mail ship in January 1932. After staying in Hong Kong for about a year, he sneaked into Shanghai, changed his name to Lin Jieshen, and rented a room with others at No. 1 Jing'an Villa on Jing'an Temple Road. His actions were secretive and his whereabouts were not discovered. Although the Japanese police station had tried its best to investigate, the case had not been solved after three years.

Arrest in the Early Morning

Until recently, the Japanese Consulate General's Office suddenly received a tip that Xu Guangyou was hiding in No. 1 Jing'an Villa, so on the morning of the 7th (yesterday) at 6 a.m., Japanese police officers Kowari and Higuchi, together with Japanese detective Iguchi and Noda from the Hongkou Police Station and more than ten Chinese and Western detectives from the Jing'an Temple Road Police Station, rushed to the front of No. 1 Jing'an Villa. They first surrounded the front and back of the building and then broke in. Xu Guangyou was sound asleep and was arrested on the spot and taken to the police station. After a brief interrogation, the Japanese police station's request was approved and Xu was transferred. It is said that he will be escorted to Kobe for interrogation soon. His wife, Oka, gave birth to a daughter only five months ago. After the incident, she cried all day and was very worried.

Stealing and Misdirecting Letters to Obtain Checks for Use

The Police Station Files Separate Lawsuits

The Court Schedules a Judgment

Hua Fu'er (transliteration), a British national who works in the Sanitation Department of the Shanghai Municipal Council and resides at No. 1283 Yu Yuan, had a letter on February 26th to a friend, Weiltai (transliteration), at No. 475 Avenue Joffre in the French Concession. A check from HSBC for 279.86 yuan was enclosed in the letter. Unexpectedly, the postman mistakenly delivered the letter to Ou Jinrong, a Ningbo native who runs a car repair shop at No. 275 Avenue Joffre. At that time, Zhang Zhizhai, a friend of Ou's (who runs a coal shop at No. 53 Rue du Père Froc), was present. Ou opened the letter and saw a check in Western characters. He asked Zhang to help him cash it. Zhang then asked Tang Yuerong to send the check to the Guohua Bank to cash the money from HSBC and share it. Now that the victim has found out about it, he reported it to the French Police Station, which sent detectives to arrest Ou and Zhang and send them to the First Special District Court for interrogation and investigation.

Now that the police station has completed the investigation, Judge Wu Fanglian conducted a trial in the Criminal Court No. 8 yesterday. First, the plaintiff Hua Fu'er stated the previous situation. When Ou Jinrong was interrogated, he confessed that after receiving the letter, he asked Zhang to cash the check and used 30 yuan after the event. Zhang Zhizhai confessed that when Ou Jinrong received the letter, he was at Ou's place. Ou asked him to ask Tang Yuerong to cash the money. Tang only gave him 60 yuan after the event. Tang said that the rest of the money had been stopped by the victim. Now, the people are willing to return the money in full and ask for leniency. The plaintiff also said that since the defendants had paid off the money, he would not pursue the crime of opening the letter.

The police lawyer Yao Zhaodi said that the police station prosecuted the first defendant for receiving stolen goods and the second defendant for theft and should be tried according to the law. After the court verified the confession, it announced the end of the debate and remanded the defendants. The judgment was rescheduled for the 13th.

Digging Up Graves for Road Construction in the City Center Discovered Poisonous Snakes

Dozens Were Killed on the Spot by Laborers

The City Center Social Affairs Bureau and Education Bureau are building a new road west of the city center. At that time, the staff staying overnight in the bureaus and nearby residents all came to watch and were shocked.

The Commercial Press Reprints the "Essentials of the Four Branches of Literature".

The Origin of the Four Branches

The term "Four Branches" in China began with Xun Xu. During the Eastern Jin Dynasty, Li Chong, the Compiler of Writings, redivided the four branches, with the Five Classics as Branch A, the various histories as Branch B, the various philosophical works as Branch C, and the poetry and prose collections as Branch D. The order of the names "Classics, History, Philosophy, and Literature" was thus established. During the Qianlong period of the Qing Dynasty, the Complete Library of the Four Branches of Literature was compiled, which used "Classics, History, Philosophy, and Literature" as the outline, recording a total of 10,291 kinds of books. After Qianlong, until the end of the Guangxu and Xuantong periods, the prosperity of famous works was enough to be a feature of Chinese culture. Dr. Sun Yat-sen's legacy was to preserve the inherent morality and promote the inherent culture. Recently, the central government has also vigorously promoted national rejuvenation. Because our ancient country with 4,000 years of culture has a lot left to us by our predecessors, we must promote and carry it forward. Only through cultural revival can the nation be revived. However, the books of the Four Branches are vast as the sea, and scholars are almost at a loss. Even if they know a little about the path of reading, it is not easy to obtain a carefully collated and annotated edition. Occasionally, a fine edition can be purchased, but it is not within the financial means of the average person, and it is impossible to purchase many fine editions at once. Therefore, it is not easy to achieve cultural普及.

The Reprints

In view of this, the Commercial Press obtained the Song edition of the Eight Thousand Scroll Tower in Hangzhou in 1920. They asked contemporary famous scholars to research and carefully select books from the Four Branches. This led to the compilation and printing of the "Essentials of the Four Branches of Literature." The old printing plates and rare editions were purchased for tens of thousands of yuan, and the cost of casting the plates reached more than 500,000 yuan. The book contains 351 kinds of books, totaling more than 11,300 volumes, with 180,000 pages, divided into 2,500 volumes. Each volume is printed with a spine for easy checking. The selected books include the Thirteen Classics with ancient annotations as a reader, the Thirteen Classics with annotations and commentaries for research, and elementary books such as "Shuowen Jiezi," "Yupian," "Guangyun," and "Jiyun." In history, in addition to the Twenty-Four Histories and "Zizhi Tongjian," it also collects ancient history, unofficial history, miscellaneous history, chronicles, biographies, memorials, geography, political books, historical reviews, tables, etc. In philosophy, in addition to the philosophers of the Zhou and Qin Dynasties, it also includes Confucian, agricultural, medical, arithmetic, divination, miscellaneous, novel, and Buddhist and Taoist classics. The book collects 14 kinds of Neo-Confucian books from the Song and Yuan Dynasties, with 92 volumes in four collections. This is because Neo-Confucianism has a significant relationship with politics and education in the last 800 years and is the foundation of self-cultivation. In literature, the "Chu Ci" crowns the separate collections, and there are 108 special collections of great masters of classical prose, poetry, and lyrics from the Han, Wei, Six Dynasties, Tang, Song, Yuan, Ming, and Qing Dynasties. The general collection begins with "Wen Xuan" and the selections of Yao and Zeng, with 23 kinds, followed by poetry and prose criticism and poetry rhymes and rhythms. The practical books of the Four Branches are almost all included here. The selected fine editions are valued for their antiquity, such as the "Five Classics with Ancient Annotations," which is based on the Song Yue Ke Xiangtai edition, and the "Fish Mysterious Machine Poetry Collection," which is based on the Northern Song edition. Some are valued for their recent editions, such as the "Four Books with Collected Annotations," which is based on the Wu engraved edition, the "Tongjian Wenxuan," which is based on the Hu engraved edition, the "Ci Lü," which is based on the En Du collated and engraved edition, and the "Dongpo Collection," which is based on the Duan Fang collated edition. Various lyric collections are mostly based on the Si Yin Zhai and Jiangcun series.

Praise from the Elders

At that time, the predecessors Yan Fansun and Liang Rengong praised it greatly. Libraries and schools in various provinces, cities, and counties should purchase it for reference. For middle school and university students, those taking higher examinations, and those studying abroad, Chinese literature and Sinology are the most important parts, and they must have a copy for research. The entire book is now being printed.

Low Price

In order to promote culture and普及 the essentials, the Commercial Press has reprinted the large five-open edition, changing the method and dividing it into twelve groups. Each group is sold in advance so that readers can choose the groups they need. The entire pre-ordered set costs 600 yuan, with each volume averaging only 24 cents. Old editions of books that cost several to dozens of yuan per volume cannot be compared with it. Even new books are not as cheap. Moreover, the money can be paid in installments, which is very easy. The bureau has printed samples and welcomes requests for them.

Wang Shuntai Woolen Shop on Nanjing Road

The business is long-established and has a good reputation. The boss, Wang Fuqing, is from Ningbo. He married a woman from his hometown, Tang, many years ago. Tang is 30 years old and their relationship is very close. Yesterday at around 2 p.m., Tang had an argument with her husband over household affairs, and a major conflict occurred. Soon after, her husband went out on business. Tang took the opportunity to secretly take a large amount of opium and commit suicide. When the family found out, they immediately hired a car and rushed her to Renji Hospital. The Post Office Purchases Publications and the Ministry Orders the Addition of Books. Implemented from April 1st.

The Ministry of Communications issued an order to the Postal Administration yesterday, saying that postal administrations in various countries can purchase books for the public through the post office to assist culture and increase postal revenue, which is a good intention. My country has a vast territory, and in addition to large cities, the public still finds it difficult to buy books. We should urgently plan to do it. The Postal Administration submitted the regulations for the post office to subscribe to publications, which have been reviewed and amended by the Ministry and approved for implementation from April 1st. However, the publications mentioned in the original submission refer specifically to newspapers and magazines and do not include books. The Ministry orders the Postal Administration to add the purchase of books so that users, bookstores, and the post office can benefit. The Postal Administration should quickly draft a plan and submit it for approval.

Two Murderers Who Killed Tang Jiapeng Appeal the Original Verdict

Tang Jiapeng, a Ningbo native who was the manager of the Rongji Game Hall in the Great World, was killed in front of the Great World at around 1 a.m. on September 18th last year. The police quickly arrested the murderers, Zhao Guangfu from Yangzhou and Zhang Xiaosizi (aka Zhang Tinggui) from Funing, and confiscated a pistol used in the murder. They were sent to the Second Special District Local Court and prosecuted for premeditated murder. After several trials, Zhao Guangfu was sentenced to life imprisonment for premeditated murder, and Zhang Xiaosizi was sentenced to 20 years in prison for assisting in premeditated murder, and both were deprived of their civil rights for life. It is reported that Zhao and Zhang were not satisfied with the original verdict and filed an appeal with the Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. The High Court is investigating the evidence and will summon witnesses to open the trial soon.

Securities:

Under Multifaceted Observation,

Bond Market Remains Stagnant

Yesterday, the Shanghai Chinese Stock Exchange saw the market stagnate after some fluctuation. Trading remained extremely thin. Several issues saw no price movement in each session. While there were still some scattered transactions on the trading floor, bids and asks often remained stuck at five cents for a long time. Increasing the price by five cents was deemed too expensive, while decreasing it by five cents was deemed too cheap. This kind of stagnation had not been seen for months. The atmosphere on the trading floor was relaxed, with few people attending. Based on this situation, it is unlikely that there will be any major changes in the short term. In this dilemma, longs lack enthusiasm, shorts dare not commit, and observation prevails as everyone waits for a change. Speculators have no opportunity to act. Yesterday, the morning opening saw strong buying in the dismissal of troops issue, while the rest saw balanced trading, with nothing noteworthy. Market prices rose slightly by one or two jiao, but some issues still saw no price movement. The second session and the afternoon opening and closing sessions were completely stagnant. Market prices in each session fluctuated, with some issues seeing no movement of even five fen. Overall, longs still seemed to be relatively stronger. The 75 issue saw relatively active trading in short-term rollovers, while the 15 and 16 issues saw some scattered demand. The rest saw mostly retail trading. Market prices overall fluctuated, with some issues seeing no price movement. Increases and decreases were between five fen and two jiao. The total trading volume was 6,898,000 yuan, including 3,000 yuan in spot trading and 6,895,000 yuan in futures trading. Yarn and Cloth:

Standard Yarn Sees Some Short Covering

The yarn market was weak in the morning and rose in the afternoon, showing a slightly calm trend. Because the factory side, in view of the yarn industry's depression, in order to maintain the factory's base, several factories unanimously united. Regarding the delivery of standard yarn, it was temporarily suspended. This stimulated the short side, which covered short positions, and the market rebounded slightly. However, actual demand is still sluggish, and pressure on the yarn market is still heavy. But the bottom has withered, making a big fall difficult.

Standard Yarn Afternoon Market Improves

In the morning market for standard yarn, prices tended to fall due to the decline of U.S. cotton, and buying was still idle. Prices for all months fell by one, two, three, and four jiao. In the afternoon, it was heard that the shorts were covering their positions due to failed yarn delivery at British factories, and the market rebounded.
